05:06:50.080 things can provide you with an extra level of legal protection to make sure that no one's going to copy your
05:06:55.920 business or come in and steal your customers. and let's talk about the differences between a trademark and a patent and if you should get both or
05:07:02.718 which one is right for you. Let's start by talking about a patent. And there are two main types of a patent. There is a utility patent and there is a design
05:07:10.240 patent. And the utility patent is only for someone that invents something new and it has to be relatively unique.
05:07:17.120 However, a utility patent can be pretty expensive to get. There's the patent search fee which is going to cost you
05:07:23.200 $540. There's also the examination fee, which is going to be another $220, as well as the application filing fee,
05:07:29.840 which is $330. And on top of that, you'll probably want to get a lawyer, and that's going to cost you around
05:07:35.680 $10,000. Now, you can do this work yourself. Jeremy, who's one of the students in my online course where I
05:07:41.840 teach people how to create unique physical products that they can sell online, he was able to file his own
05:07:47.120 utility patent. He did say that it took a lot of work and if he were to do it over again, he might actually be willing
05:07:52.878 to spend the money on a patent lawyer. So, you don't need to hire a patent lawyer, but most people that I've spoke
05:07:58.000 to end up hiring that lawyer. If you have a unique idea or invention, I would say at a minimum file for a provisional
05:08:04.080 patent. It's only $75. It's very easy to do. And then later, if you decide that you want to move forward with this
05:08:10.000 product, you can file for a full utility patent. The other option is to get a design patent. And you can get a design
05:08:16.638 patent if your product has a unique design to it. For example, the signature
05:08:21.680 Coca-Cola bottle because there's nothing from a utility standpoint that's unique about it. However, from a design
05:08:26.798 standpoint, it's something that's unique to that brand. And when you see it, you know that it's a Coca-Cola bottle. A
05:08:32.000 design patent protects the form of the product. And it's easier to get a design patent than it is a utility patent, but
05:08:38.798 it doesn't offer as much legal protection. And for carnivore electrolytes, we did not apply for a
05:08:43.840 patent because this isn't a brand new invention. There are other electrolyte powders out there. The only thing that
05:08:49.520 makes our product unique is the design itself. And that's where trademarks come in. And a trademark allows you to either
05:08:56.000 protect the graphical design. For instance, if you have a special logo, a special font, something like that that's
05:09:02.240 unique to your brand. Or you can actually protect the words themselves. For instance, Coca-Cola has a word
05:09:08.878 trademark, and that means that nobody else can use the words Coca-Cola, no matter what font or design they're
05:09:14.240 using. And out of these two options, it's a lot easier to get a design mark
05:09:19.280 than it is to get a word mark. So, if you're filing for a trademark because you want to get brand registry when

06:03:32.718 world has a UPC code. And that UPC code identifies that specific product. Now, FN skew is different because let's say I
06:03:38.878 bought a tub of laundry detergent and I decided I want to sell this on Amazon and you bought a tub of laundry
06:03:44.958 detergent and let's say that you bought the same tub of laundry detergent and you also wanted to sell it on Amazon.

06:03:56.958 of the units are your units and which of the units are my units. So, you're going to want to add on your FN SKQ to your

06:40:20.958 And now let's talk about what I think is probably the most important part of this entire video. And that is the six principles of influence. And this comes
06:40:27.120 from the book influence by Robert Chaldini. And he has studied how people can motivate people, how people can
06:40:33.360 influence people to do things for years and years. And he came up with these six
06:40:38.798 principles. And the first one is reciprocity. As humans, if someone does something nice for us, we feel
06:40:45.360 obligated. we feel compelled to do something nice for them. And you're going to want to use this principle when
06:40:51.200 you're launching your product. So think about what can you do? What's something nice you can do for your customers? Something small you can give to them
06:40:57.600 that's going to make them want to ultimately buy your product. Another way of looking at this is maybe you can do
06:41:03.120 something nice for an influencer that's going to make them want to promote your product. And an example of how you can
06:41:09.120 use reciprocity to help your product launch do better is to have influencers
06:41:14.400 on your podcast. You can create a podcast, have them on your podcast, then the influencer is likely to reciprocate
06:41:20.558 by promoting your product. Now, be careful with influence. These principles can be used for good or bad. So, make
06:41:26.718 sure when you're using these principles that you're doing it from a healthy and a good place. Principle number two is
06:41:32.320 scarcity. As humans, we want things that are scarce. If tomorrow there was a gold
06:41:37.840 bar on every single person's front doorstep, gold wouldn't seem so valuable. The reason gold is so valuable
06:41:44.000 is because it's scarce. So when you're selling your product on Amazon, one
06:41:49.120 thing that you could do is make it so that only 200 are available at a
06:41:54.718 discounted rate. And you can tell your email list, you can tell your social media, you can tell everybody there's only going to be 200 available at this
06:42:01.520 discounted rate. And that once those sell off, the price is going to go back to normal. The third principle is authority. And as humans, when someone
06:42:08.638 that's in a position of authority tells us that we should buy something, that we should do something, we're much more
06:42:13.920 likely to do it. This is another reason why you should hire or use influencers to promote your product. Influence
06:42:20.558 principle number four is consistency. As humans, we're likely to do things that we have done before again and again. And
06:42:27.680 if we make a commitment saying that we're going to do something, we're much more likely to actually follow through.
06:42:33.200 And so one way to use this principle to your advantage is get people to join a Facebook group. Get people to interact
06:42:39.040 in the Facebook group because if they're interacting in the Facebook group, they're much more likely to actually purchase your product when it comes out
06:42:45.360 because they're going to feel like that they need to stay consistent with their behavior. Principle number five is liking. We're much more likely to buy
06:42:53.280 something from someone we like. So one of the most powerful things you can do is introduce yourself to your audience.
06:43:00.478 Introduce yourself to your social media following, to your email list, maybe even make an about us video. You can
06:43:06.958 also post about us videos on your Amazon page. Principle number six is consensus, also known as social proof. When a lot
06:43:15.040 of other people like something as humans, we automatically think that we should also like it. And one of the ways
06:43:20.878 that you can use this is to get influencers talking about your product. You can also get other people in your
06:43:26.160 Facebook group or on your email list talking about how cool your product is. you can share real stories of people

07:58:48.080 is the Amazon storage fee. And this is something that a lot of people forget about, but it's very important because
07:58:54.000 Amazon actually charges you every month that you have inventory in their warehouse. And from January to September

07:59:18.160 to be making a lot of money in Q4 sales. People are buying things for the holidays and generally speaking, people
07:59:24.000 see a huge increase in sales during this month. And so, what happens is a lot of people want to send in a lot of products
07:59:29.920 into Amazon's warehouse. And to discourage people from sending in too much, they raise the fee that they
07:59:35.760 charge during this time. And the way to calculate how much your Amazon FBA storage fees are going to be is to take

07:59:47.120 example, let's say we were selling a product that is 3 in x 4 in x 5 in. That product would be 60 cubic in. Now,

08:00:05.120 in. So, we'd simply divide the cubic inches of our product, which is 60 cubic in, divided by the cubic in of 1 ft,
08:00:12.718 which is 1,728, and multiply that by the 75 cents per cubic foot that Amazon charges. And you
08:00:19.040 can see that Amazon will charge us around 2.6 cents per unit per month that we have this stored. So, if we knew that
08:00:25.280 we were going to store this product in Amazon for 4 months, that'd be 2.6 cents per month. It's going to cost us around
